<s> and did you thereupon take possession of it and charge the female prisoner with theft of the box from 6 rockingham gate <\s>
<s> and did she deny the same <\s>

<s> what was her behaviour <\s>
<s> perfectly quiet your worship <\s>
<s> she persisted in the denial <\s>
<s> do you know her <\s>
<s> is she known here <\s>
<s> no your worship they're neither of them known we ve nothing against them at all <\s>
<s> jones have you anything to ask the officer <\s>
<s> no sir thank you i ve nothing to ask him <\s>
<s> very well then go on <\s>
<s> reading from his papers and while you were taking the female prisoner did the male prisoner interpose and endeavour to hinder you in the execution of your duty and did he strike you a blow <\s>
<s> and did he say you let her go i took the box myself <\s>
<s> and did you blow your whistle and obtain the assistance of another constable and take him into custody <\s>
<s> was he violent on the way to the station and did he use bad language and did he several times repeat that he had taken the box himself <\s>
<s> snow nods did you thereupon ask him in what manner he had stolen the box <\s>
<s> and did you understand him to say he had entered the house at the invitation of young mr <\s>
<s> barthwick barthwick turning in his seat frowns at roper after midnight on easter monday and partaken of whisky and that under the influence of the whisky he had taken the box <\s>
<s> and was his demeanour throughout very violent <\s>
<s> it was very violent <\s>
<s> breaking in violent  of course it was <\s>
<s> you put your ands on my wife when i kept tellin you i took the thing myself <\s>
<s> hissing with protruded neck now you will have your chance of saying what you want to say presently <\s>
<s> have you anything to ask the officer <\s>
<s> now let us hear what the female prisoner has to say first <\s>
<s> well your worship of course i can only say what i ve said all along that i did n't take the box <\s>
<s> yes but did you know that it was taken <\s>
<s> and of course to what my husband says your worship i can't speak of my own knowledge <\s>
<s> of course i know that he came home very late on the monday night <\s>
<s> it was past one o'clock when he came in and he was not himself at all <\s>
<s> had he been drinking <\s>
<s> and was he drunk <\s>
<s> yes your worship he was almost quite drunk <\s>
<s> and did he say anything to you <\s>
<s> no your worship only to call me names <\s>
<s> and of course in the morning when i got up and went to work he was asleep <\s>
<s> and i don't know anything more about it until i came home again <\s>
<s> barthwick that s my employer your worship told me the box was missing <\s>
<s> but of course when i was shaking out my husband's coat the cigarette box fell out and all the cigarettes were scattered on the bed <\s>
<s> you say all the cigarettes were scattered on the bed <\s>
<s> to snow did you see the cigarettes scattered on the bed <\s>
<s> no your worship i did not <\s>
<s> you see he says he did n't see them <\s>
<s> well they were there for all that <\s>
<s> i can't say your worship that i had the opportunity of going round the room i had all my work cut out with the male prisoner <\s>
<s> jones well what more have you to say <\s>
<s> of course when i saw the box your worship i was dreadfully upset and i could n't think why he had done such a thing when the officer came we were having words about it because it is ruin to me your worship in my profession and i have three little children dependent on me <\s>
<s> yes yes but what did he say to you <\s>
<s> i asked him whatever came over him to do such a thing and he said it was the drink <\s>
<s> he said he had had too much to drink and something came over him <\s>
<s> and of course your worship he had had very little to eat all day and the drink does go to the head when you have not had enough to eat <\s>
<s> your worship may not know but it is the truth <\s>
<s> and i would like to say that all through his married life i have never known him to do such a thing before though we have passed through great hardships and speaking with soft emphasis i am quite sure he would not have done it if he had been himself at the time <\s>
<s> but don't you know that that is no excuse <\s>
<s> i know that it is no excuse <\s>
<s> the magistrate leans over and parleys with his clerk jack <\s>
<s> leaning over from his seat behind i say dad barthwick <\s>
<s> sheltering his mouth he speaks to roper roper you had better get up now and say that considering the circumstances and the poverty of the prisoners we have no wish to proceed any further and if the magistrate would deal with the case as one of disorder only on the part of bald constable <\s>
<s> roper shakes his head magistrate <\s>
<s> now supposing what you say and what your husband says is true what i have to consider is how did he obtain access to this house and were you in any way a party to his obtaining access <\s>
<s> you are the charwoman employed at the house <\s>
<s> yes your worship and of course if i had let him into the house it would have been very wrong of me and i have never done such a thing in any of the houses where i have been employed <\s>
<s> now let us hear what story the male prisoner makes of it <\s>
<s> who leans with his arms on the dock behind speaks in a slow sullen voice wot i say is wot my wife says <\s>

<s> and did you blow your whistle and obtain the assistance of another constable and take him into custody <\s>
<s> was he violent on the way to the station and did he use bad language and did he several times repeat that he had taken the box himself <\s>
<s> snow nods did you thereupon ask him in what manner he had stolen the box <\s>
<s> and did you understand him to say he had entered the house at the invitation of young mr <\s>

<s> and was his demeanour throughout very violent <\s>

<s> of course when i saw the box your worship i was dreadfully upset and i could n't think why he had done such a thing when the officer came we were having words about it because it is ruin to me your worship in my profession and i have three little children dependent on me <\s>
<s> yes yes but what did he say to you <\s>
<s> i asked him whatever came over him to do such a thing and he said it was the drink <\s>
<s> he said he had had too much to drink and something came over him <\s>

<s> your worship may not know but it is the truth <\s>
<s> and i would like to say that all through his married life i have never known him to do such a thing before though we have passed through great hardships and speaking with soft emphasis i am quite sure he would not have done it if he had been himself at the time <\s>

<s> and did you blow your whistle and obtain the assistance of another constable and take him into custody <\s>

<s> and did you thereupon take possession of it and charge the female prisoner with theft of the box from 6 rockingham gate <\s>

<s> did you take her into custody <\s>

<s> no sir thank you i ve nothing to ask him <\s>
<s> very well then go on <\s>
<s> reading from his papers and while you were taking the female prisoner did the male prisoner interpose and endeavour to hinder you in the execution of your duty and did he strike you a blow <\s>
<s> and did he say you let her go i took the box myself <\s>
<s> and did you blow your whistle and obtain the assistance of another constable and take him into custody <\s>
<s> was he violent on the way to the station and did he use bad language and did he several times repeat that he had taken the box himself <\s>
<s> snow nods did you thereupon ask him in what manner he had stolen the box <\s>
<s> and did you understand him to say he had entered the house at the invitation of young mr <\s>
<s> barthwick barthwick turning in his seat frowns at roper after midnight on easter monday and partaken of whisky and that under the influence of the whisky he had taken the box <\s>
<s> and was his demeanour throughout very violent <\s>
<s> it was very violent <\s>
<s> breaking in violent  of course it was <\s>
<s> you put your ands on my wife when i kept tellin you i took the thing myself <\s>
<s> hissing with protruded neck now you will have your chance of saying what you want to say presently <\s>
<s> have you anything to ask the officer <\s>
<s> now let us hear what the female prisoner has to say first <\s>
<s> well your worship of course i can only say what i ve said all along that i did n't take the box <\s>
<s> yes but did you know that it was taken <\s>
<s> and of course to what my husband says your worship i can't speak of my own knowledge <\s>
<s> of course i know that he came home very late on the monday night <\s>
<s> it was past one o'clock when he came in and he was not himself at all <\s>
<s> had he been drinking <\s>
<s> and was he drunk <\s>
<s> yes your worship he was almost quite drunk <\s>
<s> and did he say anything to you <\s>
<s> no your worship only to call me names <\s>
<s> and of course in the morning when i got up and went to work he was asleep <\s>
<s> and i don't know anything more about it until i came home again <\s>
<s> barthwick that s my employer your worship told me the box was missing <\s>
<s> but of course when i was shaking out my husband's coat the cigarette box fell out and all the cigarettes were scattered on the bed <\s>
<s> you say all the cigarettes were scattered on the bed <\s>
<s> to snow did you see the cigarettes scattered on the bed <\s>
<s> no your worship i did not <\s>
<s> you see he says he did n't see them <\s>
<s> well they were there for all that <\s>
<s> i can't say your worship that i had the opportunity of going round the room i had all my work cut out with the male prisoner <\s>
<s> jones well what more have you to say <\s>
<s> of course when i saw the box your worship i was dreadfully upset and i could n't think why he had done such a thing when the officer came we were having words about it because it is ruin to me your worship in my profession and i have three little children dependent on me <\s>
<s> yes yes but what did he say to you <\s>
<s> i asked him whatever came over him to do such a thing and he said it was the drink <\s>
<s> he said he had had too much to drink and something came over him <\s>
<s> and of course your worship he had had very little to eat all day and the drink does go to the head when you have not had enough to eat <\s>
<s> your worship may not know but it is the truth <\s>
<s> and i would like to say that all through his married life i have never known him to do such a thing before though we have passed through great hardships and speaking with soft emphasis i am quite sure he would not have done it if he had been himself at the time <\s>
<s> but don't you know that that is no excuse <\s>
<s> i know that it is no excuse <\s>
<s> the magistrate leans over and parleys with his clerk jack <\s>
<s> leaning over from his seat behind i say dad barthwick <\s>
<s> sheltering his mouth he speaks to roper roper you had better get up now and say that considering the circumstances and the poverty of the prisoners we have no wish to proceed any further and if the magistrate would deal with the case as one of disorder only on the part of bald constable <\s>
<s> roper shakes his head magistrate <\s>
<s> now supposing what you say and what your husband says is true what i have to consider is how did he obtain access to this house and were you in any way a party to his obtaining access <\s>
<s> you are the charwoman employed at the house <\s>
<s> yes your worship and of course if i had let him into the house it would have been very wrong of me and i have never done such a thing in any of the houses where i have been employed <\s>
<s> now let us hear what story the male prisoner makes of it <\s>
<s> who leans with his arms on the dock behind speaks in a slow sullen voice wot i say is wot my wife says <\s>

<s> i told her and she can tell you the same that i was goin to throw the thing into the water sooner then ave it on my mind <\s>

<s> sheltering his mouth he speaks to roper roper you had better get up now and say that considering the circumstances and the poverty of the prisoners we have no wish to proceed any further and if the magistrate would deal with the case as one of disorder only on the part of bald constable <\s>
<s> roper shakes his head magistrate <\s>
<s> now supposing what you say and what your husband says is true what i have to consider is how did he obtain access to this house and were you in any way a party to his obtaining access <\s>

<s> and did you blow your whistle and obtain the assistance of another constable and take him into custody <\s>

<s> and did you understand him to say he had entered the house at the invitation of young mr <\s>

<s> and did you blow your whistle and obtain the assistance of another constable and take him into custody <\s>

<s> and did you thereupon take possession of it and charge the female prisoner with theft of the box from 6 rockingham gate <\s>

<s> did you take her into custody <\s>

<s> no sir thank you i ve nothing to ask him <\s>
<s> very well then go on <\s>
<s> reading from his papers and while you were taking the female prisoner did the male prisoner interpose and endeavour to hinder you in the execution of your duty and did he strike you a blow <\s>
<s> and did he say you let her go i took the box myself <\s>
<s> and did you blow your whistle and obtain the assistance of another constable and take him into custody <\s>
<s> was he violent on the way to the station and did he use bad language and did he several times repeat that he had taken the box himself <\s>
<s> snow nods did you thereupon ask him in what manner he had stolen the box <\s>
<s> and did you understand him to say he had entered the house at the invitation of young mr <\s>
<s> barthwick barthwick turning in his seat frowns at roper after midnight on easter monday and partaken of whisky and that under the influence of the whisky he had taken the box <\s>
<s> and was his demeanour throughout very violent <\s>
<s> it was very violent <\s>
<s> breaking in violent  of course it was <\s>
<s> you put your ands on my wife when i kept tellin you i took the thing myself <\s>
<s> hissing with protruded neck now you will have your chance of saying what you want to say presently <\s>
<s> have you anything to ask the officer <\s>
<s> now let us hear what the female prisoner has to say first <\s>
<s> well your worship of course i can only say what i ve said all along that i did n't take the box <\s>
<s> yes but did you know that it was taken <\s>
<s> and of course to what my husband says your worship i can't speak of my own knowledge <\s>
<s> of course i know that he came home very late on the monday night <\s>
<s> it was past one o'clock when he came in and he was not himself at all <\s>
<s> had he been drinking <\s>
<s> and was he drunk <\s>
<s> yes your worship he was almost quite drunk <\s>
<s> and did he say anything to you <\s>
<s> no your worship only to call me names <\s>
<s> and of course in the morning when i got up and went to work he was asleep <\s>
<s> and i don't know anything more about it until i came home again <\s>
<s> barthwick that s my employer your worship told me the box was missing <\s>
<s> but of course when i was shaking out my husband's coat the cigarette box fell out and all the cigarettes were scattered on the bed <\s>
<s> you say all the cigarettes were scattered on the bed <\s>
<s> to snow did you see the cigarettes scattered on the bed <\s>
<s> no your worship i did not <\s>
<s> you see he says he did n't see them <\s>
<s> well they were there for all that <\s>
<s> i can't say your worship that i had the opportunity of going round the room i had all my work cut out with the male prisoner <\s>
<s> jones well what more have you to say <\s>
<s> of course when i saw the box your worship i was dreadfully upset and i could n't think why he had done such a thing when the officer came we were having words about it because it is ruin to me your worship in my profession and i have three little children dependent on me <\s>
<s> yes yes but what did he say to you <\s>
<s> i asked him whatever came over him to do such a thing and he said it was the drink <\s>
<s> he said he had had too much to drink and something came over him <\s>
<s> and of course your worship he had had very little to eat all day and the drink does go to the head when you have not had enough to eat <\s>
<s> your worship may not know but it is the truth <\s>
<s> and i would like to say that all through his married life i have never known him to do such a thing before though we have passed through great hardships and speaking with soft emphasis i am quite sure he would not have done it if he had been himself at the time <\s>
<s> but don't you know that that is no excuse <\s>
<s> i know that it is no excuse <\s>
<s> the magistrate leans over and parleys with his clerk jack <\s>
<s> leaning over from his seat behind i say dad barthwick <\s>
<s> sheltering his mouth he speaks to roper roper you had better get up now and say that considering the circumstances and the poverty of the prisoners we have no wish to proceed any further and if the magistrate would deal with the case as one of disorder only on the part of bald constable <\s>
<s> roper shakes his head magistrate <\s>
<s> now supposing what you say and what your husband says is true what i have to consider is how did he obtain access to this house and were you in any way a party to his obtaining access <\s>
<s> you are the charwoman employed at the house <\s>
<s> yes your worship and of course if i had let him into the house it would have been very wrong of me and i have never done such a thing in any of the houses where i have been employed <\s>
<s> now let us hear what story the male prisoner makes of it <\s>
<s> who leans with his arms on the dock behind speaks in a slow sullen voice wot i say is wot my wife says <\s>

<s> i told her and she can tell you the same that i was goin to throw the thing into the water sooner then ave it on my mind <\s>

<s> sheltering his mouth he speaks to roper roper you had better get up now and say that considering the circumstances and the poverty of the prisoners we have no wish to proceed any further and if the magistrate would deal with the case as one of disorder only on the part of bald constable <\s>
<s> roper shakes his head magistrate <\s>
<s> now supposing what you say and what your husband says is true what i have to consider is how did he obtain access to this house and were you in any way a party to his obtaining access <\s>

<s> and did you blow your whistle and obtain the assistance of another constable and take him into custody <\s>

<s> and did you understand him to say he had entered the house at the invitation of young mr <\s>

<s> and did you blow your whistle and obtain the assistance of another constable and take him into custody <\s>

<s> and did you thereupon take possession of it and charge the female prisoner with theft of the box from 6 rockingham gate <\s>

<s> did you take her into custody <\s>

<s> no sir thank you i ve nothing to ask him <\s>
<s> very well then go on <\s>
<s> reading from his papers and while you were taking the female prisoner did the male prisoner interpose and endeavour to hinder you in the execution of your duty and did he strike you a blow <\s>
<s> and did he say you let her go i took the box myself <\s>
<s> and did you blow your whistle and obtain the assistance of another constable and take him into custody <\s>
<s> was he violent on the way to the station and did he use bad language and did he several times repeat that he had taken the box himself <\s>
<s> snow nods did you thereupon ask him in what manner he had stolen the box <\s>
<s> and did you understand him to say he had entered the house at the invitation of young mr <\s>
<s> barthwick barthwick turning in his seat frowns at roper after midnight on easter monday and partaken of whisky and that under the influence of the whisky he had taken the box <\s>
<s> and was his demeanour throughout very violent <\s>
<s> it was very violent <\s>
<s> breaking in violent  of course it was <\s>
<s> you put your ands on my wife when i kept tellin you i took the thing myself <\s>
<s> hissing with protruded neck now you will have your chance of saying what you want to say presently <\s>
<s> have you anything to ask the officer <\s>
<s> now let us hear what the female prisoner has to say first <\s>
<s> well your worship of course i can only say what i ve said all along that i did n't take the box <\s>
<s> yes but did you know that it was taken <\s>
<s> and of course to what my husband says your worship i can't speak of my own knowledge <\s>
<s> of course i know that he came home very late on the monday night <\s>
<s> it was past one o'clock when he came in and he was not himself at all <\s>
<s> had he been drinking <\s>
<s> and was he drunk <\s>
<s> yes your worship he was almost quite drunk <\s>
<s> and did he say anything to you <\s>
<s> no your worship only to call me names <\s>
<s> and of course in the morning when i got up and went to work he was asleep <\s>
<s> and i don't know anything more about it until i came home again <\s>
<s> barthwick that s my employer your worship told me the box was missing <\s>
<s> but of course when i was shaking out my husband's coat the cigarette box fell out and all the cigarettes were scattered on the bed <\s>
<s> you say all the cigarettes were scattered on the bed <\s>
<s> to snow did you see the cigarettes scattered on the bed <\s>
<s> no your worship i did not <\s>
<s> you see he says he did n't see them <\s>
<s> well they were there for all that <\s>
<s> i can't say your worship that i had the opportunity of going round the room i had all my work cut out with the male prisoner <\s>
<s> jones well what more have you to say <\s>
<s> of course when i saw the box your worship i was dreadfully upset and i could n't think why he had done such a thing when the officer came we were having words about it because it is ruin to me your worship in my profession and i have three little children dependent on me <\s>
<s> yes yes but what did he say to you <\s>
<s> i asked him whatever came over him to do such a thing and he said it was the drink <\s>
<s> he said he had had too much to drink and something came over him <\s>
<s> and of course your worship he had had very little to eat all day and the drink does go to the head when you have not had enough to eat <\s>
<s> your worship may not know but it is the truth <\s>
<s> and i would like to say that all through his married life i have never known him to do such a thing before though we have passed through great hardships and speaking with soft emphasis i am quite sure he would not have done it if he had been himself at the time <\s>
<s> but don't you know that that is no excuse <\s>
<s> i know that it is no excuse <\s>
<s> the magistrate leans over and parleys with his clerk jack <\s>
<s> leaning over from his seat behind i say dad barthwick <\s>
<s> sheltering his mouth he speaks to roper roper you had better get up now and say that considering the circumstances and the poverty of the prisoners we have no wish to proceed any further and if the magistrate would deal with the case as one of disorder only on the part of bald constable <\s>
<s> roper shakes his head magistrate <\s>
<s> now supposing what you say and what your husband says is true what i have to consider is how did he obtain access to this house and were you in any way a party to his obtaining access <\s>
<s> you are the charwoman employed at the house <\s>
<s> yes your worship and of course if i had let him into the house it would have been very wrong of me and i have never done such a thing in any of the houses where i have been employed <\s>
<s> now let us hear what story the male prisoner makes of it <\s>
<s> who leans with his arms on the dock behind speaks in a slow sullen voice wot i say is wot my wife says <\s>

<s> i told her and she can tell you the same that i was goin to throw the thing into the water sooner then ave it on my mind <\s>

<s> sheltering his mouth he speaks to roper roper you had better get up now and say that considering the circumstances and the poverty of the prisoners we have no wish to proceed any further and if the magistrate would deal with the case as one of disorder only on the part of bald constable <\s>
<s> roper shakes his head magistrate <\s>
<s> now supposing what you say and what your husband says is true what i have to consider is how did he obtain access to this house and were you in any way a party to his obtaining access <\s>

<s> and did you blow your whistle and obtain the assistance of another constable and take him into custody <\s>

<s> and did you understand him to say he had entered the house at the invitation of young mr <\s>

<s> and did you blow your whistle and obtain the assistance of another constable and take him into custody <\s>

<s> and did you thereupon take possession of it and charge the female prisoner with theft of the box from 6 rockingham gate <\s>

<s> did you take her into custody <\s>

<s> no sir thank you i ve nothing to ask him <\s>
<s> very well then go on <\s>
<s> reading from his papers and while you were taking the female prisoner did the male prisoner interpose and endeavour to hinder you in the execution of your duty and did he strike you a blow <\s>
<s> and did he say you let her go i took the box myself <\s>
<s> and did you blow your whistle and obtain the assistance of another constable and take him into custody <\s>
<s> was he violent on the way to the station and did he use bad language and did he several times repeat that he had taken the box himself <\s>
<s> snow nods did you thereupon ask him in what manner he had stolen the box <\s>
<s> and did you understand him to say he had entered the house at the invitation of young mr <\s>
<s> barthwick barthwick turning in his seat frowns at roper after midnight on easter monday and partaken of whisky and that under the influence of the whisky he had taken the box <\s>
<s> and was his demeanour throughout very violent <\s>
<s> it was very violent <\s>
<s> breaking in violent  of course it was <\s>
<s> you put your ands on my wife when i kept tellin you i took the thing myself <\s>
<s> hissing with protruded neck now you will have your chance of saying what you want to say presently <\s>
<s> have you anything to ask the officer <\s>
<s> now let us hear what the female prisoner has to say first <\s>
<s> well your worship of course i can only say what i ve said all along that i did n't take the box <\s>
<s> yes but did you know that it was taken <\s>
<s> and of course to what my husband says your worship i can't speak of my own knowledge <\s>
<s> of course i know that he came home very late on the monday night <\s>
<s> it was past one o'clock when he came in and he was not himself at all <\s>
<s> had he been drinking <\s>
<s> and was he drunk <\s>
<s> yes your worship he was almost quite drunk <\s>
<s> and did he say anything to you <\s>
<s> no your worship only to call me names <\s>
<s> and of course in the morning when i got up and went to work he was asleep <\s>
<s> and i don't know anything more about it until i came home again <\s>
<s> barthwick that s my employer your worship told me the box was missing <\s>
<s> but of course when i was shaking out my husband's coat the cigarette box fell out and all the cigarettes were scattered on the bed <\s>
<s> you say all the cigarettes were scattered on the bed <\s>
<s> to snow did you see the cigarettes scattered on the bed <\s>
<s> no your worship i did not <\s>
<s> you see he says he did n't see them <\s>
<s> well they were there for all that <\s>
<s> i can't say your worship that i had the opportunity of going round the room i had all my work cut out with the male prisoner <\s>
<s> jones well what more have you to say <\s>
<s> of course when i saw the box your worship i was dreadfully upset and i could n't think why he had done such a thing when the officer came we were having words about it because it is ruin to me your worship in my profession and i have three little children dependent on me <\s>
<s> yes yes but what did he say to you <\s>
<s> i asked him whatever came over him to do such a thing and he said it was the drink <\s>
<s> he said he had had too much to drink and something came over him <\s>
<s> and of course your worship he had had very little to eat all day and the drink does go to the head when you have not had enough to eat <\s>
<s> your worship may not know but it is the truth <\s>
<s> and i would like to say that all through his married life i have never known him to do such a thing before though we have passed through great hardships and speaking with soft emphasis i am quite sure he would not have done it if he had been himself at the time <\s>
<s> but don't you know that that is no excuse <\s>
<s> i know that it is no excuse <\s>
<s> the magistrate leans over and parleys with his clerk jack <\s>
<s> leaning over from his seat behind i say dad barthwick <\s>
<s> sheltering his mouth he speaks to roper roper you had better get up now and say that considering the circumstances and the poverty of the prisoners we have no wish to proceed any further and if the magistrate would deal with the case as one of disorder only on the part of bald constable <\s>
<s> roper shakes his head magistrate <\s>
<s> now supposing what you say and what your husband says is true what i have to consider is how did he obtain access to this house and were you in any way a party to his obtaining access <\s>
<s> you are the charwoman employed at the house <\s>
<s> yes your worship and of course if i had let him into the house it would have been very wrong of me and i have never done such a thing in any of the houses where i have been employed <\s>
<s> now let us hear what story the male prisoner makes of it <\s>
<s> who leans with his arms on the dock behind speaks in a slow sullen voice wot i say is wot my wife says <\s>

<s> i told her and she can tell you the same that i was goin to throw the thing into the water sooner then ave it on my mind <\s>

<s> sheltering his mouth he speaks to roper roper you had better get up now and say that considering the circumstances and the poverty of the prisoners we have no wish to proceed any further and if the magistrate would deal with the case as one of disorder only on the part of bald constable <\s>
<s> roper shakes his head magistrate <\s>
<s> now supposing what you say and what your husband says is true what i have to consider is how did he obtain access to this house and were you in any way a party to his obtaining access <\s>

<s> and did you blow your whistle and obtain the assistance of another constable and take him into custody <\s>

<s> and did you understand him to say he had entered the house at the invitation of young mr <\s>

<s> and did you blow your whistle and obtain the assistance of another constable and take him into custody <\s>

<s> and did you thereupon take possession of it and charge the female prisoner with theft of the box from 6 rockingham gate <\s>

<s> did you take her into custody <\s>

<s> no sir thank you i ve nothing to ask him <\s>
<s> very well then go on <\s>
<s> reading from his papers and while you were taking the female prisoner did the male prisoner interpose and endeavour to hinder you in the execution of your duty and did he strike you a blow <\s>
<s> and did he say you let her go i took the box myself <\s>
<s> and did you blow your whistle and obtain the assistance of another constable and take him into custody <\s>
<s> was he violent on the way to the station and did he use bad language and did he several times repeat that he had taken the box himself <\s>
<s> snow nods did you thereupon ask him in what manner he had stolen the box <\s>
<s> and did you understand him to say he had entered the house at the invitation of young mr <\s>
<s> barthwick barthwick turning in his seat frowns at roper after midnight on easter monday and partaken of whisky and that under the influence of the whisky he had taken the box <\s>
<s> and was his demeanour throughout very violent <\s>
<s> it was very violent <\s>
<s> breaking in violent  of course it was <\s>
<s> you put your ands on my wife when i kept tellin you i took the thing myself <\s>
<s> hissing with protruded neck now you will have your chance of saying what you want to say presently <\s>
<s> have you anything to ask the officer <\s>
<s> now let us hear what the female prisoner has to say first <\s>
<s> well your worship of course i can only say what i ve said all along that i did n't take the box <\s>
<s> yes but did you know that it was taken <\s>
<s> and of course to what my husband says your worship i can't speak of my own knowledge <\s>
<s> of course i know that he came home very late on the monday night <\s>
<s> it was past one o'clock when he came in and he was not himself at all <\s>
<s> had he been drinking <\s>
<s> and was he drunk <\s>
<s> yes your worship he was almost quite drunk <\s>
<s> and did he say anything to you <\s>
<s> no your worship only to call me names <\s>
<s> and of course in the morning when i got up and went to work he was asleep <\s>
<s> and i don't know anything more about it until i came home again <\s>
<s> barthwick that s my employer your worship told me the box was missing <\s>
<s> but of course when i was shaking out my husband's coat the cigarette box fell out and all the cigarettes were scattered on the bed <\s>
<s> you say all the cigarettes were scattered on the bed <\s>
<s> to snow did you see the cigarettes scattered on the bed <\s>
<s> no your worship i did not <\s>
<s> you see he says he did n't see them <\s>
<s> well they were there for all that <\s>
<s> i can't say your worship that i had the opportunity of going round the room i had all my work cut out with the male prisoner <\s>
<s> jones well what more have you to say <\s>
<s> of course when i saw the box your worship i was dreadfully upset and i could n't think why he had done such a thing when the officer came we were having words about it because it is ruin to me your worship in my profession and i have three little children dependent on me <\s>
<s> yes yes but what did he say to you <\s>
<s> i asked him whatever came over him to do such a thing and he said it was the drink <\s>
<s> he said he had had too much to drink and something came over him <\s>
<s> and of course your worship he had had very little to eat all day and the drink does go to the head when you have not had enough to eat <\s>
<s> your worship may not know but it is the truth <\s>
<s> and i would like to say that all through his married life i have never known him to do such a thing before though we have passed through great hardships and speaking with soft emphasis i am quite sure he would not have done it if he had been himself at the time <\s>
<s> but don't you know that that is no excuse <\s>
<s> i know that it is no excuse <\s>
<s> the magistrate leans over and parleys with his clerk jack <\s>
<s> leaning over from his seat behind i say dad barthwick <\s>
<s> sheltering his mouth he speaks to roper roper you had better get up now and say that considering the circumstances and the poverty of the prisoners we have no wish to proceed any further and if the magistrate would deal with the case as one of disorder only on the part of bald constable <\s>
<s> roper shakes his head magistrate <\s>
<s> now supposing what you say and what your husband says is true what i have to consider is how did he obtain access to this house and were you in any way a party to his obtaining access <\s>
<s> you are the charwoman employed at the house <\s>
<s> yes your worship and of course if i had let him into the house it would have been very wrong of me and i have never done such a thing in any of the houses where i have been employed <\s>
<s> now let us hear what story the male prisoner makes of it <\s>
<s> who leans with his arms on the dock behind speaks in a slow sullen voice wot i say is wot my wife says <\s>

<s> i told her and she can tell you the same that i was goin to throw the thing into the water sooner then ave it on my mind <\s>

<s> sheltering his mouth he speaks to roper roper you had better get up now and say that considering the circumstances and the poverty of the prisoners we have no wish to proceed any further and if the magistrate would deal with the case as one of disorder only on the part of bald constable <\s>
<s> roper shakes his head magistrate <\s>
<s> now supposing what you say and what your husband says is true what i have to consider is how did he obtain access to this house and were you in any way a party to his obtaining access <\s>

<s> and did you blow your whistle and obtain the assistance of another constable and take him into custody <\s>

<s> and did you understand him to say he had entered the house at the invitation of young mr <\s>
